currency_value_evolution_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            #has_modifier = has_financial_center
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = currency_value_evolution_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = currency_value_evolution_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_global_variable_list = currency_value_evolution_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = money_value_dif_1_final
                    max = 15
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_global_variable_list = {
                            name = currency_value_evolution_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = currency_value_evolution_list
    }
}
independent_economies_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
			}
			is_revolutionary = no
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = independent_economies_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = independent_economies_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_global_variable_list = independent_economies_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = money_value_in_gold
                    max = 100
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_global_variable_list = {
                            name = independent_economies_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = independent_economies_list
    }
}
dependent_economies_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			is_revolutionary = no
			NOT = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
			}
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = dependent_economies_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = dependent_economies_list

                    max = 100
                    check_range_bounds = no

    }
}
money_supply_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
          is_reference_type = 1
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = money_supply_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = money_supply_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_global_variable_list = money_supply_variable_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = total_money_supply
                    max = 10
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_global_variable_list = {
                            name = money_supply_variable_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = money_supply_variable_list
    }
}
national_capacity_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			not = {
				or = {
					market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
					is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
				}
			}
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = national_capacity_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = national_capacity_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
                remove_modifier = global_monetary_reference
            }
            clear_global_variable_list = national_capacity_variable_list_ordered_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = list_before_order
                order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
                min = 0
                max = 10
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_global_variable_list = {
                        name = national_capacity_variable_list_ordered_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = reference_currency_list_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = reference_currency_country_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = reference_currency_list_1
                order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
                min = 0
                position = 1
                max = 1
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = reference_currency_country_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            every_in_list = {
                variable = reference_currency_country_1
                if = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = global_monetary_reference
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
is_subject_list = {  #local
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            or = {
                is_subject_of = root
                #
                #is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
            }
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = is_subject_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = is_subject_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = is_subject_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = prestige
                    max = 10
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = is_subject_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = is_subject_list
    }
}

exports_imports_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
			export_value_in_currency > 0
			import_value_in_currency > 0
			global_country_ranking < 20
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = exports_imports_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = exports_imports_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_global_variable_list = exports_imports_variable_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = trade_balance_convert_gold #trade_balance_in_gold
                    max = 20
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_global_variable_list = {
                            name = exports_imports_variable_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = exports_imports_variable_list
    }
}

#power
national_capacity_power_1_list = {
	clear_variable_list = national_capacity_power_1
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			not = {
				or = {
					market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
					is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
				}
			}
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = national_capacity_power_1
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = { 
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = national_capacity_power_1
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                } 
            }
            clear_variable_list = national_capacity_power_1_ordered_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = list_before_order
                order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
                min = 0
                max = 5
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = national_capacity_power_1_ordered_1
                        target = prev
                    } 
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = national_capacity_power_1_country_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = national_capacity_power_1_ordered_1
                order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
                min = 0
                position = 1
                max = 1
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = national_capacity_power_1_country_1
                        target = prev
                    } 
                }
            }  
            clear_variable_list = national_capacity_power_2_country_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = national_capacity_power_1_ordered_1
                order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
                min = 1
                position = 2
                max = 2
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = national_capacity_power_2_country_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            } 
            clear_variable_list = national_capacity_power_3_country_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = national_capacity_power_1_ordered_1
                order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
                min = 2
                position = 3
                max = 3
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = national_capacity_power_3_country_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            } 
        }
    }
}

                        name = evolution_currency_value_1_ordered_1
                        target = prev
                    } 
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = evolution_currency_value_1_country_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = evolution_currency_value_1_ordered_1
                order_by = money_value_dif_1_final
                min = 0
                position = 1
                max = 1
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = evolution_currency_value_1_country_1
                        target = prev
                    } 
                }
            }  
            clear_variable_list = evolution_currency_value_2_country_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = evolution_currency_value_1_ordered_1
                order_by = money_value_dif_1_final
                min = 1
                position = 2
                max = 2
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {

                    }

                min = 2

central_bank_debt_variable_list = {
	#changement de princuipe ce n'azi plus la dette de la bank qui compter
	#modifier l'odre de pays acheter en premier à l'avenir avec un score ?

    every_country = {
        limit = {
			gold_loaned_to_central_bank < total_debt_80 #tout les pays avec une dette non comblé à au minimum 80% sont éligible
			central_bank_metal_reserves_state_to_ensure_the_conversion_pourcent < 0.75 #donc besoin investissement

			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			not = {
				#market_owner_is_root
				any_scope_state = {
					is_production_method_active = {
						building_type = building_bank
						production_method = pm_no_metal_consuption
					}
					not = {
						is_production_method_active = {
							building_type = building_bank
							production_method = pm_no_subject_currency_type
						}
					}
				}
				has_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			} 
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = central_bank_debt_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = central_bank_debt_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_global_variable_list = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
			ordered_in_list = {
				variable = list_before_order
				order_by = remaining_debt
				max = 100
				check_range_bounds = no
				root = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = {
						name = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
        }
        clear_variable_list = central_bank_debt_variable_list
    }
}
country_index_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_financial_center
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = country_index_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = country_index_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
                remove_modifier = global_financial_power
            }
            clear_global_variable_list = country_index_variable_list_ordered_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = list_before_order
                order_by = country_indice_in_gold #country_indice
                max = 10
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_global_variable_list = {
                        name = country_index_variable_list_ordered_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = financial_power_list_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = financial_power_country_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = financial_power_list_1
                order_by = country_indice_in_gold #country_indice
                min = 0
                position = 1
                max = 1
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = financial_power_country_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            every_in_list = {
                variable = financial_power_country_1
                if = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = global_financial_power
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = country_index_variable_list
    }
}

		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = privat_bank_variable_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = private_bank_funds_per_private_bank_add_foreign_debt
					max = 100
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_variable_list = {
							name = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = privat_bank_variable_list
	}
}

#dinar
dinar_currency_law_list = {
	clear_variable_list = dinar_currency_law_list
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_dinar_currency
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
		}
		remove_modifier = dinar_leading_currency_type
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = dinar_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = dinar_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = dinar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = dinar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = dinar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = dinar_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = dinar_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = dinar_currency_list
	}
	if = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_dinar_currency
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			}
			remove_modifier = dinar_leading_currency_type
		}
	}
}

	clear_variable_list = eco_tuareg_ouguiya_currency_law_list
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_eco_tuareg_ouguiya_currency
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
		}
		remove_modifier = eco_tuareg_ouguiya_leading_currency_type
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = eco_tuareg_ouguiya_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = eco_tuareg_ouguiya_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = eco_tuareg_ouguiya_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = eco_tuareg_ouguiya_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = eco_tuareg_ouguiya_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = eco_tuareg_ouguiya_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = eco_tuareg_ouguiya_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = eco_tuareg_ouguiya_currency_list
	}
	if = {

				root = {

					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = gulden_south_german_gulden_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}

				variable = gulden_south_german_gulden_currency_law_list_ordered_1

		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_lira_ducato_currency
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
		}
		remove_modifier = lira_ducato_leading_currency_type
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = lira_ducato_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = lira_ducato_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = lira_ducato_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = lira_ducato_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = lira_ducato_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = lira_ducato_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = lira_ducato_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = lira_ducato_currency_list
	}
	if = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_lira_ducato_currency
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			}
			remove_modifier = lira_ducato_leading_currency_type
		}
	}
}

				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = peso_colombian_peso_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = peso_colombian_peso_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = peso_colombian_peso_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = peso_colombian_peso_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = peso_colombian_peso_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = peso_colombian_peso_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = peso_colombian_peso_currency_list
	}
	if = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_peso_colombian_peso_currency
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			}
			remove_modifier = peso_colombian_peso_leading_currency_type
		}
	}
}

					}

					variable = list_before_order

					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no

		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = spe_dong_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = spe_dong_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = spe_dong_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = spe_dong_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = spe_dong_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = spe_dong_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = spe_dong_currency_list
	}
	if = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_spe_dong_currency
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			}

		}

thaler_prussian_thaler_currency_law_list = {
	clear_variable_list = thaler_prussian_thaler_currency_law_list
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_thaler_prussian_thaler_currency
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
		}
		remove_modifier = thaler_prussian_thaler_leading_currency_type
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = thaler_prussian_thaler_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = thaler_prussian_thaler_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = thaler_prussian_thaler_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = thaler_prussian_thaler_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = thaler_prussian_thaler_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = thaler_prussian_thaler_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = thaler_prussian_thaler_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = thaler_prussian_thaler_currency_list

#dinar
dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			stockpiling_dinar_state > 0
		}
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = dinar_c_total_stokpile
					max = 10
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_variable_list = {
							name = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = money_supply_variable_list
	}
}

		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order

				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = peso_cuban_peso_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = peso_cuban_peso_c_total_stokpile
					max = 10
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_variable_list = {
							name = peso_cuban_peso_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
							target = prev

#test_1 -> pas sup nb de bc
test_1_c_global_stokpile_variable_list = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = test_1_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = test_1_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = test_1_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity_in_gold
					max = 100
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_variable_list = {
							name = test_1_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = money_supply_variable_list
	}
}

#test_6-> pas sup nb de faillite tout type
test_6_c_global_stokpile_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
			#has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
			}
			is_revolutionary = no
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = test_6_c_global_stokpile_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = test_6_c_global_stokpile_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_global_variable_list = test_6_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = central_bank_metal_reserves_state_to_ensure_the_conversion_pourcent
                    max = 100
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_global_variable_list = {
                            name = test_6_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = test_6_c_global_stokpile_variable_list
    }
}
#test_7-> pas sup nb de faillite tout type
test_7_c_global_stokpile_variable_list = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_weak_currency = yes
			market_owner_is_root_4 = yes
		}
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = test_7_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_7
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = test_7_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_7
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = test_7_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_test_7
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = { value = 0 subtract = money_value_in_gold }
					max = 100
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_variable_list = {
							name = test_7_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_test_7
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = test_7_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_7
	}
}

#test_10-> pas sup nb de faillite tout type
test_10_c_global_stokpile_variable_list = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes #has bc
			has_financial_center = yes #has fc
			remaining_debt > 0
			market_owner_is_root_4 = yes
			central_bank_metal_reserves_state_to_ensure_the_conversion_pourcent < 0.75
			not = {
				has_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			}
		}
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = test_10_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_10
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = test_10_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_10
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = test_10_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_test_10
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = central_bank_metal_reserves_state_25 #{ value = 0 subtract = money_value_in_gold }
					max = 100
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_variable_list = {
							name = test_10_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_test_10
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = test_10_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_10
	}
}

                target = prev

        }
    } 
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = test_14_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_14
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = test_14_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_test_14
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = var:economic_instability_count #{ value = 0 subtract = money_value_in_gold }
					max = 100
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_variable_list = {
							name = test_14_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_test_14
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = test_14_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_14
	}
}
#test_15-> pas sup nb de faillite tout type
test_15_c_global_stokpile_variable_list = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				has_modifier = has_central_bank
				has_modifier = has_financial_center
			}
			or = {
				var:economic_instability_count >= 1
				var:currency_crisis >= 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy >= 1
				var:financial_crash >= 1
				var:economic_crisis >= 1 


				
				var:economic_instability_count_count = 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy_count = 1
				var:currency_crisis_count = 1
				var:financial_crash_count = 1
				var:economic_crisis_count = 1 
			}
			not = {
				var:country_bankruptcy = 1
			}
		}
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = test_15_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_15
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = test_15_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_15
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = test_15_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_test_15
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = economic_instability_count #{ value = 0 subtract = money_value_in_gold }
					max = 100
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = test_15_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_test_15
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = test_15_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_15
	}
}
#test_16-> pas sup nb de faillite tout type
test_16_c_global_stokpile_variable_list = {
	every_country = {
		limit = { 
			or = {
				has_modifier = has_central_bank
				has_modifier = has_financial_center
			}
			not = {
				or = {
					market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
					is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = test_16_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_16
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = test_16_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_16
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = test_16_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_test_16
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = money_value_in_gold #{ value = 0 subtract = money_value_in_gold }
					max = 100
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = test_16_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_test_16
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = test_16_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_test_16
	}
}
